Disulfur difluoride,Dsufur dnuonde,S $\mathrm { S } _ { 2 } \mathrm { F } _ { 2 }$ , exists as mixture of two isomers, as shown below. The equi-sts s mxture of two 1somers,as sown below.Ihe eu librium is catalyzed by metal fluorides:ibr ium is catalyaed by metal luorides

$$
\begin{array}{l} \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} - \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} ^ {F} \xrightarrow {} \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} - \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} ^ {F} \\ \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} - \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} ^ {F} \xrightarrow {} \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} - \underset {F} {\mathrm {S}} ^ {F} \end{array} \tag {6.99}
$$
